The room are big and clean. The staff were very helpful and cheerful too. The most amazing discovery for me is that the restaurant served delicious,fresh and healthy dishes. We ate there every night and it was really enjoyable. The steamed fish was fresh and the size suitable for the two of us. Amazing chef.üëç There were many different types of spa pools out in the open including a heated swimming pool. There were also private spa with heated floor. After the spa, we have some free fruits and drinks inside the spa area. The whole spa were very well staff and clean. The only setback is that the water doesn‚Äôt have any smell so I don‚Äôt know if it is real hot springs underground water so it could just heated piped water. There were also some ongoing construction activities in this development area. The rooms however were well insulated so little noise if we closed our windows and doors. But overall, we have a really enjoyable 2 nights stay in this new hotel. We would come back next time to this hotel if we visit Taibaishan again which closed the top two stations during our stay due to weather conditions.

msg:For the May Day trip to Taibai Mountain, Qilin Mansion saved my mood (I had booked Taibai Meihao Lizhi Hotel 10 days in advance, but I was furious when communicating with her and almost cancelled the trip to Taibai. My previous slogan of choosing Meihao as the first choice for business trips was severely slapped in the face. I will tell you more about the details when I have the chance. In short, I will never go to Taibai Mountain Meihao Lizhi Hotel again in this lifetime. The biggest problem with changing hotels at the last minute is that the price is too high. Thanks to the customer service lady of Ctrip who understood my situation and mood and gave me the biggest subsidy, which reduced my cost. Thank you very much!). Back to the point, we arrived at the hotel around 3:30 in the afternoon. It was drizzling. There were 3 or 4 security guards holding umbrellas at the entrance of the hotel to help direct parking and hold umbrellas. Their attitude was very good üëç. After checking in, we entered the room (a parent-child room booked by a family of three). The room was large enough, the bathtub was deep and clean, and there was a tent next to it. It felt very good. After checking the time, we quickly changed clothes and went to the hot spring (accommodating guests can soak in the hot spring an unlimited number of times). The hot spring has two major indoor and outdoor areas. It was drizzling and the outdoor area felt beautiful. Although it was the May Day holiday, we could basically find empty pools outdoors, which had both beautiful scenery and a certain degree of privacy. We took a red wine bath and an angelica bath, and took a bunch of beautiful photos of the baby. By the way, there is also a swimming pool outdoors for swimming. The indoor pool is a large pool with massages of various water currents. The water bar has self-service fruits and unlimited drinks. We also played three games of billiards with a temporary opponent (1 win and 2 losses üòÇ). In short, I give the hot spring 5 points. In addition, the hotel's buffet breakfast impressed me the most. It is no exaggeration to say that it is comparable to the standard of a 5-star hotel, comparable to Sheraton. I just don't know if it is of this standard on weekdays. If it is, it would be quite amazing. The only drawback is that the price is a bit expensive, but the hotels around the scenic area are not cheap during the short holiday! That's all.

posted:Posted April 7, 2024
msg:The hotel is clean and hygienic. The rooms are well-lit and ventilated. Children also like the smart home. The service attitude of the service staff at the front desk, guest rooms, hot springs, and restaurants is also very good. But there are two points that are not very satisfactory:
1. The safety that hot spring hotels need to pay attention to is not very good. Some places have anti-slip mats outside the hot spring pool and some do not (the hotel said that they have customized anti-slip mats but have not been delivered yet), which caused my family to slip and fall in places without anti-slip mats. However, the hotel quickly brought ice compresses, iodine and Yunnan Baiyao to help deal with it. But this happened on the night of check-in, which made it impossible to continue to soak in the hot spring. The subsequent mountain climbing trip had to be cancelled and we had to go home, which was a bit disappointing.
2. You can't take the elevator directly to the hot spring when you check in. It is not very convenient to queue up at the entrance of the hot spring every time. You can refer to other hotels to directly apply for wristbands when checking in. It will be much more convenient to enter and exit the hot spring freely during your stay.
3. Children like to play on the outdoor slide, but around 11:20 in the morning, the staff saw that the other children had left and only my child was playing, so they turned off the water and stopped him from playing. The business hours in the morning are from 10 to 12 o'clock. It cannot be closed just because there are fewer people playing. Later, around 11:30, a parent came with his child and asked why it was closed. The staff opened it again.
Combined with the previous two things, the overall experience was not very good.
